***набрасывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a> (18699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросать.html>наброса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросать.html>наброса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sketch, to draw an outline <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to sketch, to outline, to draft
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrásyvatʹ</b> plan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to outline a plan</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to jot down</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросок.html>набро́сок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nabrósok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nabrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw <i>(on, over)</i>, to slip on, to slip over</li></ol>

***набрасываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a> (16233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrásyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall <i>(upon, on)</i>, to pounce <i>(on)</i>, to attack, to assault, to go <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrásyvatʹsja</b> na jedú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fall on the food</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrásyvatʹsja</b> na knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pounce on a book; snatch at a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrásyvatʹsja</b> na predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pounce on the offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down <i>(on)</i>, to jump <i>(on)</i>, to jump all over</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наки́дываться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nakídyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***набрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a> (2341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набирать.html>набира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set up, to compose, to type (a text on a computer)</li>
<li>to gather; to pick; to collect; to assemble; to take (a lot of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гриб.html>грибо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> korzínu gribóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gather a basket of mushrooms</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заказ.html>зака́зов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> zakázov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take a lot of orders</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> uglja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take on coal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take on; to enlist, to recruit; to engage; to enrol, to make up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завод.html>заво́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> rabóčix na zavód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take on workers at a factory</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:учащийся.html>уча́щихся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:техникум.html>те́хникум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> učáščixsja v téxnikum</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enrol students (for technical school)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труппа.html>тру́ппу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> trúppu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make up a (e.g. theatre) company</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>idiomatic</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́на</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> nómer (telefóna)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dial a (telephone) number</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:темп.html>те́мпы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> tɛ́mpy rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to achieve a good pace of work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рота.html>рот</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> vodý v rot</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep mum (figurative)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высоту́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> vysotú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to climb, to gain height / altitude</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹ</b> skórostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gather / pick up speed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***набраться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a> (5793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набираться.html>набира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather, to accumulate, to come up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́лись</a></b> кое-каки́е <a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>nabrálisʹ</b> koje-kakíje sberežénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I've made/accumulated some savings</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be there
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желающий.html>жела́ющих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:немного.html>немно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">želájuščix nemnógo <b>nabrálosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were few volunteers (if any)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collect, to summon up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:храбрость.html>хра́брости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹsja</b> xrábrosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pluck/summon up one's courage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹsja</b> dúxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹsja</b> nóvyx sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">summon up fresh energy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наглость.html>на́глости</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> (+ )</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹsja</b> náglosti i (+ )</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take the audacity (+ to )</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to learn, to pick up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ума́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrátʹsja</b> umá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn sense; grow wise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грубый.html>гру́бых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чек</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gde on <b>nabrálsja</b> étix grúbyx slovéček?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">where did he pick up those rude words?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be full, to tank up <i>(on alcohol)</i>, to load up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>набра́лся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ty opjátʹ <b>nabrálsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you are full again!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрать.html>набра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***набрести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набрести.html>набрести́</a> (17045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брести.html>брести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрести.html>набрести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">набреда́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find, to come across <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit upon (an idea) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gather <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of many people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набрести.html>набрело́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabreló</b> mnógo naródu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a large crowd gathered</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">набреда́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabredátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is rare.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набросать.html>наброса́ть</a> (13910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросать.html>броса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросать.html>наброса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrosátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sketch, to draw an outline <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to sketch, to outline, to draft
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набросать.html>наброса́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrosátʹ</b> plan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to outline a plan</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to jot down</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a> (11711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrósitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасывать.html>набра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw <i>(on, over)</i>, to slip on, to slip over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrósitʹ</b> (na sebjá) palʹtó (býstro)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slip on a coat; slip a coat over one's shoulders</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a> (8371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrósitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрасываться.html>набра́сываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall <i>(upon, on)</i>, to pounce <i>(on)</i>, to attack, to assault, to go <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́силась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáka <b>nabrósilasʹ</b> na menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the dog went for [pounced on / at] me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall <i>(upon, on)</i>, to pounce <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrósitʹsja</b> na jedú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fall on the food</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrósitʹsja</b> na knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pounce on a book; snatch at a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наброситься.html>набро́ситься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nabrósitʹsja</b> na predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pounce on the offer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come down <i>(on)</i>, to jump <i>(on)</i>, to jump all over</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набросить.html>набро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:набрякнуть.html>набря́кнуть</a> (21172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брякнуть.html>бря́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brjáknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набрякнуть.html>набря́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nabrjáknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">набряка́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swell up from moisture</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">набряка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabrjakátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is rare.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:набухнуть.html>набу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nabúxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***наваждение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наваждение.html>наважде́ние</a> (12721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Church Slavonic <span class="Cyrs" lang="cu">наваждениѥ</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="tr Latn">navaždenije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Old Church Slavonic <span class="Cyrs" lang="cu">навадити</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="tr Latn">navaditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваждение.html>наважде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navaždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваждение.html>наважде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваждение.html>наважде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваждение.html>наважде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delusion, hallucination</li>
<li>obsession</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a> (31933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naválivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put <i>(on)</i>, to heap up <i>(on)</i>, to pile <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́чу</a> (испражня́ться)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naválivatʹ</b> kúču (ispražnjátʹsja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dump a load</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to load <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to pile up</li>
<li>to come in crowds</li></ol>

***наваливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a> (14532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naválivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lean all one's weight <i>(upon)</i>, to bring all one's weight to bear <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>вёсла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naválivatʹsja</b> na vjósla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull hard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overburden, to weigh heavily <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>naválivajutsja</b> nóvyje objázannosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is being loaded/taxed/charged/saddled/lumbered with new responsibilities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na menjá <b>naválivajetsja</b> kúča del</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am being snowed under with work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come <i>(over)</i>, to be seized <i>(with)</i>, to have an attack <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>naválivajetsja</b> toská</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is having a sudden attack of depression (of the blues)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naválivatʹsja</b> na jedú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall on the food</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go to work <i>(on)</i>, to attack, to dig <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учебник.html>уче́бники</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naválivatʹsja</b> na učébniki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hit the books</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">lean</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:налегать.html>налега́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nalegátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***навалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a> (11546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливать.html>нава́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put <i>(on)</i>, to heap up <i>(on)</i>, to pile <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сверху.html>све́рху</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svérxu <b>navalíli</b> tjažólyj kámenʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they put a heavy stone on top</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стол</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́чу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na stol <b>navalíli</b> kúču knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they heaped up (piled) books on the table</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́чу</a> (испражни́ться)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navalítʹ</b> kúču (ispražnítʹsja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dump a load</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to load <i>(with)</i>, to saddle <i>(with)</i>, to lumber <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>navalíli</b> nóvyje objázannosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was loaded/taxed/charged/saddled/lumbered with new responsibilities</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pile up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mnógo snégu <b>navalílo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there are huge piles of snow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колено.html>коле́но</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snégu <b>navalílo</b> po koléno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the snow piled up knee-deep</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come in crowds
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ду</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naródu <b>navalílo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the place was overcrowded/packed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***навалиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a> (5807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наваливаться.html>нава́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lean all one's weight <i>(upon)</i>, to bring all one's weight to bear <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весло.html>вёсла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navalítʹsja</b> na vjósla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull hard</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́сь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navalísʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pull away!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overburden, to weigh heavily <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>navalílisʹ</b> nóvyje objázannosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was loaded/taxed/charged/saddled/lumbered with new responsibilities</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́ча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na menjá <b>navalílasʹ</b> kúča del</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am snowed under with work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come <i>(over)</i>, to be seized <i>(with)</i>, to have an attack <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тоска.html>тоска́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na nevó <b>navalílasʹ</b> toská</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he had a sudden attack of depression (of the blues)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navalítʹsja</b> na jedú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall on the food</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go to work <i>(on)</i>, to attack, to dig <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:навалиться.html>навали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учебник.html>уче́бники</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>navalítʹsja</b> na učébniki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hit the books</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навалить.html>навали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наварить.html>навари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">navarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навар.html>нава́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">navár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навар.html>нава́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навар.html>нава́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навар.html>нава́ров</a></b>)
</p>

<li>broth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> profit</li></ol>
